<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">антисове́т(ский)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">antisovét(skij)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-щик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ščik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:антисоветчик.html>антисове́тчик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">antisovétčik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:антисоветчик.html>антисове́тчика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:антисоветчик.html>антисове́тчики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:антисоветчик.html>антисове́тчиков</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">антисове́тчица</b>)
</p>

***антитело.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:антитело.html>антитело</a> (23553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1895. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">анти-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">anti-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тело.html>те́ло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">télo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">anticorps</i> or  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Antikörper</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:антитело.html>антите́ло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">antitélo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:антитело.html>антите́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:антитело.html>антитела́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:антитело.html>антите́л</a></b>)

***аорта.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аорта.html>ао́рта</a> (23155)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀορτή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aortḗ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the arteries springing from the heart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀορτέω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aortéō</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, lengthened form of <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀείρω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aeírō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I lift, raise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аорта.html>ао́рта</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aórta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аорта.html>ао́рты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аорта.html>ао́рты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аорта.html>ао́рт</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> aorta

***апатия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:апатия.html>апа́тия</a> (20079)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀπάθεια</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">apátheia</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">freedom from suffering</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀπαθής</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">apathḗs</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">without feeling</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">a-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">without</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πάθος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">páthos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апатия.html>апа́тия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">apátija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апатия.html>апа́тии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апатия.html>апа́тии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апатия.html>апа́тий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>apathy, indifference</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***апеллировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:апеллировать.html>апелли́ровать</a> (23884)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">apellieren</i> (variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">appellieren</i>) + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апеллировать.html>апелли́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">apellírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to appeal <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to address, to appeal <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to make reference <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to appeal '<i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:апеллировать.html>апелли́ровать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разум.html>ра́зуму</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>apellírovatʹ</b> k rázumu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to appeal to reason</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:апеллировать.html>апелли́ровать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лучший.html>лу́чшим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вствам</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>apellírovatʹ</b> k lúčšim čúvstvam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">appeal to smb's better nature</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:апельсин.html>апельси́н</a> (7402)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">appelsien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pomme de Sine</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Chinese apple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апельсин.html>апельси́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">apelʹsín</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апельсин.html>апельси́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апельсин.html>апельси́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апельсин.html>апельси́нов</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:апельсин.html>апельси́н</a></strong><sup>*</sup></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Informal.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li>orange tree
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горький.html>го́рький</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:апельсин.html>апельси́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">górʹkij <b>apelʹsín</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>Citrus aurantium</i>) <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/marmalade_orange" class="extiw" title="w:marmalade orange">marmalade orange</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>orange (fruit)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долька.html>до́лька</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:апельсин.html>апельси́на</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dólʹka <b>apelʹsína</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">orange segment</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ть</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свинья.html>свинья́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:апельсин.html>апельси́нах</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">(ponimátʹ) kak svinʹjá v <b>apelʹsínax</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(to know as much about something) as a pig about pineapples</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">(to understand) like a pig in oranges</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аплодировать.html>аплоди́ровать</a> (10550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аплодировать.html>аплоди́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aplodírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зааплодировать.html>зааплоди́ровать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поаплоди́ровать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to applaud, to cheer, to clap
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зритель.html>зри́тели</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:аплодировать.html>аплоди́ровали</a></b> жонглёру.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zríteli <b>aplodírovali</b> žongljóru.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The audience applauded the juggler.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аплодисменты.html>аплодисме́нты</a> (6280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аплодисменты.html>аплодисме́нты</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aplodisménty</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аплодисменты.html>аплодисме́нтов</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>applause, clapping, cheers
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурный.html>бу́рные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:аплодисменты.html>аплодисме́нты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">búrnyje aplodisménty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">storm of applause, loud cheers, wild applause</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встреча́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:аплодисменты.html>аплодисме́нтами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vstrečátʹ aplodisméntami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to greet with cheers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:аплодисменты.html>аплодисме́нты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pod aplodisménty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to the applause</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:апломб.html>апло́мб</a> (26405)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">aplomb</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апломб.html>апло́мб</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aplómb</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апломб.html>апло́мба</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апломб.html>апло́мбы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апломб.html>апло́мбов</a></b>)
